***одолевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одолевать.html>одолева́ть</a> (9969)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолеть.html>одоле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odolétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолевать.html>одолева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odolevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолеть.html>одоле́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to overpower, to subdue
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одолевать.html>одолева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:враг.html>врага́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odolevátʹ</b> vragá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overpower the enemy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seize, to overcome
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одолевать.html>одолева́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:любопытство.html>любопы́тство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>odolevájet</b> ljubopýtstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is beset by curiosity</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cope, to manage</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побеждать.html>побежда́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobeždátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подавлять.html>подавля́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podavljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересиливать.html>переси́ливать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peresílivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покорять.html>покоря́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pokorjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">снеда́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">snedátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оси́ливать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osílivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***одолеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одолеть.html>одоле́ть</a> (5890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">одолѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odolěti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*odolěti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолеть.html>одоле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odolétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолевать.html>одолева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to overcome, to overpower, to conquer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:одолеть.html>одоле́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:враг.html>врага́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>odolétʹ</b> vragá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overpower the enemy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seize, to overcome
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одолеть.html>одоле́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сон</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>odolél</b> son</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was overcome by sleepiness</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cope, to manage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никак.html>ника́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одолеть.html>одоле́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on nikák ne <b>odoléjet</b> étu knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he cannot get through this book</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:победить.html>победи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobedítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пересилить.html>переси́лить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peresílitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осилить.html>оси́лить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">osílitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***одолжённый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжённый</a> (11181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odolžónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odolžítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***одолживший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́вший</a> (11181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***одолжить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́ть</a> (11181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долг.html>долг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dolg</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odolžítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одалживать.html>ода́лживать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lend <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to allow to be used temporarily</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to borrow <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to receive (something) temporarily</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The difference between "to lend" and "to borrow" is determined by the context and the usage of prepositions and cases, e.g. "he lent me (some) money" is "<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>" ("<a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>" is a dative case) and "he has borrowed (some) money from me" is "<a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одолжить.html>одолжи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a>" ("<a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a>" is used with the genitive case).</li>
<li>The object of lending/borrowing is normally in the accusative but can also be in the genitive case, especially in the negative clauses.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одолжение.html>одолже́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odolžénije</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">favour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одуванчик.html>одува́нчик</a> (8672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одуванчик.html>одува́нчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oduvánčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одуванчик.html>одува́нчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одуванчик.html>одува́нчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одуванчик.html>одува́нчиков</a></b>)

***одуматься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:одуматься.html>оду́маться</a> (16540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dúmatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одуматься.html>оду́маться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">odúmatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">оду́мываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to think better of it, to change one's mind</li>
<li>to come to one's senses
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заставить.html>заста́вить</a> кого́-л <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одуматься.html>оду́маться</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zastávitʹ kovó-l <b>odúmatʹsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to bring smb to smb's senses</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наконец.html>наконе́ц</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одуматься.html>оду́мается</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kogdá že oná nakonéc <b>odúmajetsja</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">when will she come to her senses, after all?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:одуматься.html>оду́маться</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> ...</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne uspél on <b>odúmatʹsja</b>, kak oní ...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">before he knew it, they ...</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуреть.html>дуре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">durétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одуреть.html>одуре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odurétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одурь.html>о́дурь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ódurʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одурь.html>о́дури</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одурь.html>о́дури</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одуреть.html>о́дурей</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожесточенный.html>ожесточённый</a> (8773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожесточенный.html>ожесточённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ožestočónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ожесточи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ožestočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожесточенный.html>ожесточённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ožestočónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hardhearted, bitter, embittered, hardened</li>
<li>desperate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ожесточенный.html>ожесточённое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сопротивление.html>сопротивле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ožestočónnoje</b> soprotivlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fierce/violent/desperate resistance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ожесточенный.html>ожесточённый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спора.html>спор</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ožestočónnyj</b> spor</i> ― <span class="e-translation">heated controversy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ожесточа́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ožestočátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ожесточи́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ožestočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожесточение.html>ожесточе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ožestočénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жестокость.html>жесто́кость</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žestókostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оживать.html>ожива́ть</a> (10144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожить.html>ожи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ožítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживать.html>ожива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oživátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожить.html>ожи́ть</a></b>)

***оживить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оживить.html>оживи́ть</a> (11513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">живи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">živítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживить.html>оживи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oživítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживлять.html>оживля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring back to life</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to revive, to bring back (something that has been lost or forgotten)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to imbue physical or emotional energy into (e.g. into a person or street)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to improve the appearance of (e.g. a building)</li></ol>

***оживленно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оживленный.html>оживлённо</a> (10087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживленный.html>оживлённо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oživljónno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживленный.html>оживлённо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oživljónno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживленный.html>оживлённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oživljónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>excited, animated</li>
<li>boisterous</li>
<li>lively
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оживленный.html>оживлённая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:беседа.html>бесе́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oživljónnaja</b> beséda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">lively conversation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оживленный.html>оживлённые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>oživljónnyje</b> úlicy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">busy streets</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***оживлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оживлять.html>оживля́ть</a> (18286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживить.html>оживи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oživítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживлять.html>оживля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oživljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживить.html>оживи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bring back to life</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to revive, to bring back (of something that has been lost or forgotten)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to imbue physical or emotional energy (ex. into a person, a street)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to improve the appearance (ex. of a building)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживлять.html>оживля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oživljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидать.html>ожида́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ožidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидание.html>ожида́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ožidánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидание.html>ожида́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидание.html>ожида́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ожидание.html>ожида́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>expectation, waiting, pending
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зал.html>за́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидание.html>ожида́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zál ožidánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">waiting room</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
